# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
fib_rec(n)

fib_iter(n) ^HD2CCSkv

O(2^n)

O(n) ^WPF1BM9g

fib_iter(n)
    if( n <= 1 ) return n
    for( i = 2 ; i < n ; i++ )
        sum = prev + curr;
        prev = curr;
        curr = sum;
return cyrr; ^QdBekL0i

fib_rec(n)
    if( n <= 1 ) 
         return n;
     return fib_rec(n - 1) + fib_rec(n - 2); ^TB47ns6P

memo[N + 1] = {-1, ... ,-1};
fib_memo(n)
     if( n <= 1 ) 
         return n;
     if( memo[n] == -1 )
          memo[n] = fib_memo(n - 1) + fib_memo(n - 2);
     return memo[n]; ^NiKzIZLy

fib_tab(n)
    if( n <= 1 ) return n
    tab[N]; tab[0] = 0; tab[1] = 1;
    for( i = 2 ; i < n ; i++ )
        tab[i] = tab[i - 1] + tab[i - 2];
return tab[N]; ^dzCPjCad
